--- Commit Message ---
LU-14980 mdd: mdd_layout_swap() to follow tx-lock rule

i.e. start transaction first, then take local (osd) locks
on the objects involved.

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2021-09-03 06:01:02.000000000) ---
Patch Set 3: Code-Review+1

It looks like there is a "lustre/tests/racer/file_swap.sh" program, but it is *not* being run as part of any racer test, there isn't even an option to run it.

It would make sense to conditionally add file_swap.sh to lustre/tests/racer/racer.sh, and add a version check to lustre/tests/racer.sh so that this is only run for MDS versions that include this patch.
